#New regex 1: PPOSWRES->MRES  e.g -650A>T; instad of > an arrow is also permitted,  see (e.g. PMID: 19568425)
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;])(?P<pos>([*+-])?[1-9][0-9]*(?:\s?[+-]\s?[1-9][0-9]*)?)\s{0,1}(?P<wt_res>[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJ])\s{0,1}(?:-{0,2}>|→)\s{0,1}(?P<mut_res>[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX])(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))[CASE_SENSITIVE]
#New regex 1a: nt PPOS:WRES-MRES  e.g nt 1494: G-A
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;])nt (?P<pos>([*+-])?[1-9][0-9]*(?:\s?[+-]\s?[1-9][0-9]*)?)\s{0,1}:\s{0,1}(?P<wt_res>[ATGC])\s{0,1}(?:-{0,2}>?|→?)\s{0,1}(?P<mut_res>[ATGC])(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))[CASE_SENSITIVE]
#New regex 2: PPOSWRES/MRES e.g. -123A/T or 123A\T, also for protein mentions
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;])(?P<pos>([*+-])?[1-9][0-9]*(?:\s?[+-]\s?[1-9][0-9]*)?)\s{0,1}(?P<wt_res>[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*])\s{0,1}(?:/|\\)\s{0,1}(?P<mut_res>([CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*]|[Ss]top))(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))[CASE_SENSITIVE]
#New regex 3: +/- 123Ala[/\]Tyr (Almost the same as regex2, but for three letter amino acids only)
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;])(?P<pos>[1-9][0-9]*)\s{0,1}(?P<wt_res>(?:CYS|ILE|SER|GLN|MET|ASN|PRO|LYS|ASP|THR|PHE|ALA|GLY|HIS|LEU|ARG|TRP|VAL|GLU|TYR|ASX|GLX|XLE|TER|STP|STOP|TERM))\s{0,1}(?:/|\\)\s{0,1}(?P<mut_res>(?:CYS|ILE|SER|GLN|MET|ASN|PRO|LYS|ASP|THR|PHE|ALA|GLY|HIS|LEU|ARG|TRP|VAL|GLU|TYR|ASX|GLX|XLE|TER|STP|STOP|TERM|X))(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))
#New regex 4a: in general used to describe allelic variants (e.g., M/V470, M/V 470)
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;])(?P<wt_res>[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*])/(?P<mut_res>[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*])\s?(?P<pos>[1-9][0-9]*)(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))[CASE_SENSITIVE]
#New regex 4b: in general used to describe allelic variants (e.g., Met/Val470, Met/Val 470)
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;])(?P<wt_res>(?:CYS|ILE|SER|GLN|MET|ASN|PRO|LYS|ASP|THR|PHE|ALA|GLY|HIS|LEU|ARG|TRP|VAL|GLU|TYR|ASX|GLX|XLE|TER|STP|STOP|TERM))/(?P<mut_res>(?:CYS|ILE|SER|GLN|MET|ASN|PRO|LYS|ASP|THR|PHE|ALA|GLY|HIS|LEU|ARG|TRP|VAL|GLU|TYR|ASX|GLX|XLE|TER|STP|STOP|TERM))\s?(?P<pos>[1-9][0-9]*)(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))
#New regex 4c: G12 to A
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;])(?P<wt_res>[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*])\s?(?P<pos>[1-9][0-9]*) to (?P<mut_res>[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*])(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))[CASE_SENSITIVE]
#New regex 5a: WRES-->MRES at PPOS
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;])(?P<wt_res>(?:[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*]|CYS|ILE|SER|GLN|MET|ASN|PRO|LYS|ASP|THR|PHE|ALA|GLY|HIS|LEU|ARG|TRP|VAL|GLU|TYR|ASX|GLX|XLE|TER|STP|STOP|TERM))\s{0,1}(?:-{0,2}>|→)\s{0,1}(?P<mut_res>(?:[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*]|CYS|ILE|SER|GLN|MET|ASN|PRO|LYS|ASP|THR|PHE|ALA|GLY|HIS|LEU|ARG|TRP|VAL|GLU|TYR|ASX|GLX|XLE|TER|STP|STOP|TERM)) at (?P<pos>[1-9][0-9]*)(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))
# WRES-->MRES at PPOS (generated from mutationfinder WRES-->MRES at _position_ PPOS)
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;\-])(?P<wt_res>(CYS|ILE|SER|GLN|MET|ASN|PRO|LYS|ASP|THR|PHE|ALA|GLY|HIS|LEU|ARG|TRP|VAL|GLU|TYR|ASX|GLX|XLE|TER|STP)|(GLUTAMINE|GLUTAMIC ACID|LEUCINE|VALINE|ISOLEUCINE|LYSINE|ALANINE|GLYCINE|ASPARTATE|METHIONINE|THREONINE|HISTIDINE|ASPARTIC ACID|ARGININE|ASPARAGINE|TRYPTOPHAN|PROLINE|PHENYLALANINE|CYSTEINE|SERINE|GLUTAMATE|TYROSINE|TERM|STOP|AMBER|UMBER|OPAL))(?:-{0,2}>|→)(?P<mut_res>(CYS|ILE|SER|GLN|MET|ASN|PRO|LYS|ASP|THR|PHE|ALA|GLY|HIS|LEU|ARG|TRP|VAL|GLU|TYR|ASX|GLX|XLE|TER|STP)|(GLUTAMINE|GLUTAMIC ACID|LEUCINE|VALINE|ISOLEUCINE|LYSINE|ALANINE|GLYCINE|ASPARTATE|METHIONINE|THREONINE|HISTIDINE|ASPARTIC ACID|ARGININE|ASPARAGINE|TRYPTOPHAN|PROLINE|PHENYLALANINE|CYSTEINE|SERINE|GLUTAMATE|TYROSINE|TERM|STOP|AMBER|UMBER|OPAL)) at (?P<pos>[1-9][0-9]*)(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))
# WRES was substituted by MRES at residue PPOS (added from Nala testcase)
(?:^|[\s\(\[\'"/,;\-])(?P<wt_res>(CYS|ILE|SER|GLN|MET|ASN|PRO|LYS|ASP|THR|PHE|ALA|GLY|HIS|LEU|ARG|TRP|VAL|GLU|TYR|ASX|GLX|XLE|TER|STP)|(GLUTAMINE|GLUTAMIC ACID|LEUCINE|VALINE|ISOLEUCINE|LYSINE|ALANINE|GLYCINE|ASPARTATE|METHIONINE|THREONINE|HISTIDINE|ASPARTIC ACID|ARGININE|ASPARAGINE|TRYPTOPHAN|PROLINE|PHENYLALANINE|CYSTEINE|SERINE|GLUTAMATE|TYROSINE|TERM|STOP|AMBER|UMBER|OPAL)) was substituted by (?P<mut_res>(CYS|ILE|SER|GLN|MET|ASN|PRO|LYS|ASP|THR|PHE|ALA|GLY|HIS|LEU|ARG|TRP|VAL|GLU|TYR|ASX|GLX|XLE|TER|STP)|(GLUTAMINE|GLUTAMIC ACID|LEUCINE|VALINE|ISOLEUCINE|LYSINE|ALANINE|GLYCINE|ASPARTATE|METHIONINE|THREONINE|HISTIDINE|ASPARTIC ACID|ARGININE|ASPARAGINE|TRYPTOPHAN|PROLINE|PHENYLALANINE|CYSTEINE|SERINE|GLUTAMATE|TYROSINE|TERM|STOP|AMBER|UMBER|OPAL)) at residue (?P<pos>[1-9][0-9]*)(?=([.,\s)\]\'":;\-?!/]|$))

###Number (simple) = (?P<pos>[1-9][0-9]*)
###Mut-res = (?P<mut_res>[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*])
###Wt-res = (?P<wt_res>[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*])
###(?P<wt_res>[CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX]|[Cc]ys|[Ii]le|[Ss]er|[Gg]ln|[Mm]et|[Aa]sn|[Pp]ro|[Ll]ys|[Aa]sp|[Tt]hr|[Pp]he|[Aa]la|[Gg]ly|[Hh]is|[Ll]eu|[Aa]rh|[Tt]rp|[Vv]al|[Gg]lu|[Tt]yr|[Gg]lutamine|[Gg]lutamic [Aa]cid|[Ll]eucine|[Vv]aline|[Ii]soleucine|[Ll]ysine|[Aa]lanine|[Gg]lycine|[Aa]spartate|[Mm]ethionine|[Tt]hreonine|[Hh]istidine|[Aa]spartic [Aa]cid|[Aa]rginine|[Aa]sparagine|[Tt]ryptophan|[Pp]roline|[Pp]henylalanine|[Cc]ysteine|[Ss]erine|[Gg]lutamate|[Tt]yrosine|[Ss]top|[Tt]erm?)
###(?P<mut_res>([CISQMNPKDTFAGHLRWVEYBZJX*]|[Cc]ys|[Ii]le|[Ss]er|[Gg]ln|[Mm]et|[Aa]sn|[Pp]ro|[Ll]ys|[Aa]sp|[Tt]hr|[Pp]he|[Aa]la|[Gg]ly|[Hh]is|[Ll]eu|[Aa]rh|[Tt]rp|[Vv]al|[Gg]lu|[Tt]yr|[Gg]lutamine|[Gg]lutamic [Aa]cid|[Ll]eucine|[Vv]aline|[Ii]soleucine|[Ll]ysine|[Aa]lanine|[Gg]lycine|[Aa]spartate|[Mm]ethionine|[Tt]hreonine|[Hh]istidine|[Aa]spartic [Aa]cid|[Aa]rginine|[Aa]sparagine|[Tt]ryptophan|[Pp]roline|[Pp]henylalanine|[Cc]ysteine|[Ss]erine|[Gg]lutamate|[Tt]yrosine|[Ss]top|[Tt]erm?))
